Short Answer
Yesâ€”technically the very same â€œsee â†’ decide â†’ actâ€ loop can drive a fully-automated game bot.
Whether you should do it (from an ethical / ToS standpoint) is another matterâ€”but from a purely engineering angle itâ€™s 100 % feasible.

1 Â· How the Vision-Loop Maps onto a Game Bot
PC-Control 2.0 Layer	Game-Bot Role	Extra Demands in Games
Screen Capture (mss)	Grab the frame buffer at 30-144 Hz	Very low latency; ideally GPU copy (NVFBC, DXGI)
Perception
âˆ™ OCR / Icon match
âˆ™ Template match
âˆ™ Object detection (YOLOv8)	Detect HP bars, buffs, mobs, UI buttons	Needs sub-10 ms per frame; icon match alone yet may be too slow
Decision

Safety / Timeout	Anti-loop & anti-ban logic	Randomized delays, human-like variance
2 Â· Key Technical Hurdles
Challenge	Notes & Mitigations
Frame Rate	mss or pyautogui.screenshot tops out at ~30 Hz. Use platform hooks:
â€¢ Windows â†’ DXGI desktop duplication
â€¢ Linux â†’ XShm, Wayland pipewire
Image Recognition Speed	Static template-match isnâ€™t enough for 3-D scenes. Use
â€¢ lightweight CNN/YOLO (8-bit quant) on GPU
â€¢ OR memory read (cheats) but that breaks ToS outright
Input Timing	Simulated HID events may be rate-limited (125â€“250 Hz). For APM-heavy games inject low-level events (SendInput, XTest)
Anti-Cheat	Easy Anti-Cheat, BattleEye, etc. detect:
â€“ suspicious process names
â€“ overlay capture
â€“ WinAPI injection. Use only on single-player / open-source titles to stay legal.
Human-like Randomness	Jitter cursor Â±3 px, random 50â€“120 ms delays, vary pathing.
3 Â· Viability vs Feasibility Snapshot
Target	Viable?	Feasible?	Why / Why Not
Idle / clicker game	â˜…â˜…â˜…â˜…â˜…	â˜…â˜…â˜…â˜…â˜…	Low FPs, deterministic UIâ€”easy

4 Â· Minimal Viable Bot Stack (Proof of Concept)
Capture â€” DXGI dup @ 60 Hz (â‰ˆ2â€“3 ms / frame)

â†’ end-to-end latency â‰ˆ 10â€“12 ms, enough for many PvE games.

5 Â· Legal / Ethical Check
ToS: Most online games prohibit any automation. Ban risk â†’ 100 %.

Good Playground:
Open-source engines (e.g. OpenRA), emulators, or your own Unity builds.

Safety: Never test on your main account. Use throw-away VMs / alt accounts.

Bottom line
Can you build it with the PC-Control + Planner loop? Yes.

Will it work everywhere? Works great for slow or single-player titles; real-time PvP with anti-cheat demands more invasive (memory-read) methodsâ€”which cross both technical and ethical lines.
If you stick to legal sandboxes, the very architecture we designed (vision loop + FSM + retry) is already 70 % of a game-bot; just swap â€œInstallerAgentâ€ with â€œCombatAgentâ€ and tighten latency.

(And if/when you want to prototype, start on an open-source gameâ€”same pipeline, zero ban risk.)
